				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Die Schöpfung, Hob.XXI:2 (Haydn, Joseph)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="wp_header">
<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>34 movements in 3 parts
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1796-1798
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Die Schöpfung
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">The Creation
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Haydn,_Joseph" title="Category:Haydn, Joseph">Haydn, Joseph</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Opus/Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">Op./Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://archive.org/stream/JosephHaydnThematisch-bibliographischesWerkverzeichnis/Hoboken1-3#page/n907/mode/2up">Hob.XXI:2</a></span>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>IJH 378
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>34 movements in 3 parts
<dl><dt><ul><li>Part I
</li></ul>
</dt><dd>1. Prelude: <i>Die Vorstellung des Chaos</i>. Largo (C minor)
</dd><dd>2. Aria and Chorus: <i>Nun schwanden vor dem heiligen Strahle</i>. Andante (A major)
</dd><dd>3. Recitative: <i>Und Gott machte das Firmament</i>. Recit - Allegro assai (C major)
</dd><dd>4. Solo and Chorus: <i>Mit Staunen sieht das Wunderwerk</i>. Allegro (C major)
</dd><dd>5. Recitative: <i>Und Gott sprach: Es sammle sich das Wasser</i> (B-flat major)
</dd><dd>6. Aria: <i>Rollend in schäumenden Wellen</i>. Allegro assai (D minor)
</dd><dd>7. Recitative: <i>Und Gott sprach: Es bringe die Erde Gras hervor</i> (B-flat major)
</dd><dd>8. Aria: <i>Nun beut die Flur das frische Grün</i>. Andante (B-flat major)
</dd><dd>9. Recitative: <i>Und die himmlischen Heerscharen verkündigten</i> (A minor)
</dd><dd>10. Chorus: <i>Stimmt an die Saiten</i>. Vivace (D major)
</dd><dd>11. Recitative: <i>Und Gott sprach: Es sei'n Lichter an der Feste des Himmels</i> (D minor)
</dd><dd>12. Accompanied recitative: <i>In vollem Glanze steiget jetzt die Sonne</i>. Andante (D major)
</dd><dd>13. Trio and Chorus: <i>Die Himmel erzählen die Ehre Gottes</i>. Allegro (C major)
</dd></dl>
<dl><dt><ul><li>Part II
</li></ul>
</dt><dd>14. Recitative: Und Gott sprach: Es bringe das Wasser in der Fülle hervor (C major)
</dd><dd>15. Aria: Auf starkem Fittiche schwinget sich der Adler stolz. Moderato (F major)
</dd><dd>16. Recitative and Aria: Und Gott schuf große Walfisch. Recit. - Poco adagio (D minor)
</dd><dd>17. Recitative: Und die Engel rührten ihr' unsterblichen Harfen (A minor)
</dd><dd>18. Trio: In holder Anmut stehn. Moderato (A major)
</dd><dd>19. Trio and Chorus: Der Herr ist groß in seiner Macht. Vivace (A major)
</dd><dd>20. Recitative: Und Gott sprach: Es bringe die Erde hervor lebende Geschöpfe (D major)
</dd><dd>21. Accompanied recitative: Gleich öffnet sich der Erde Schoß. Presto (B-flat major)
</dd><dd>22. Aria: Nun scheint in vollem Glanze der Himmel. Maestoso (D major)
</dd><dd>23. Recitative: Und Gott schuf den Menschen (C major)
</dd><dd>24. Aria: Mit Würd' und Hoheit angetan. Andante (C major)
</dd><dd>25. Recitative: Und Gott sah jedes Ding (B-flat major)
</dd><dd>26. Chorus: Vollendet ist das große Werk. Vivace (B-flat major)
</dd><dd>27. Trio: Zu dir, o Herr, blickt alles auf. Poco adagio (E-flat major)
</dd><dd>28. Chorus: Vollendet ist das große Werk. Vivace (B-flat major)
</dd></dl>
<dl><dt><ul><li>Part III
</li></ul>
</dt><dd>29. Accompanied recitative: Aus Rosenwolken bricht. Largo (E major)
</dd><dd>30. Duet and Chorus: Von deiner Güt', o Herr und Gott. Adagio (C major)
</dd><dd>31. Recitative: Nun ist die erste Pflicht erfüllt (E-flat major)
</dd><dd>32. Duet: Holde Gattin, dir zur Seite. Adagio (E-flat major)
</dd><dd>33. Recitative: O glücklich Paar, und glücklich immerfort (B-flat major)
</dd><dd>34. Trio and Chorus: Singt dem Herren alle Stimmen! Andante - Allegro (B-flat major)
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Year/Date of Composition</span><span class="ms555">Y/D of Comp.</span>
</th>
<td>1796-1798
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Perf<span class="mh555">ormance</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1798-04-29 (private performance)<br />1799-03-17 in Vienna: Burgtheater (public performance)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Pub<span class="mh555">lication</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1800
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Librettist
</th>
<td>Baron <a href="/wiki/Category:Swieten,_Gottfried_van" title="Category:Swieten, Gottfried van">Gottfried van Swieten</a> (1733-1803)
<dl><dd>after the Bible (Genesis and Psalms) and <a href="/wiki/Category:Milton,_John" title="Category:Milton, John">John Milton</a> <i><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Paradise_Lost" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Paradise Lost">(Paradise Lost)</a></i>
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Language
</th>
<td>German and English
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Composer Time Period</span><span class="ms555">Comp. Period</span>
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Classical" title="Category:Classical">Classical</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Piece Style
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Classical_style" title="Category:Classical style">Classical</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Instrumentation
</th>
<td>voices, mixed chorus, orchestra <div class="expandline" style="background-color:#E8E8E8;margin-left:0;margin-top:0;padding:0">
<dl><dd><i>Cast:</i>
<dl><dd>Gabriel/Eve<br />Uriel<br />Raphael/Adam
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd><i>Voices:</i>
<dl><dd>soprano, tenor, bass, mixed chorus (SATB)
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd><i>Orchestra:</i>  
<dl><dd>3 flutes, 2 oboes, 2 clarinets (B<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>, C), 2 bassoons, contrabassoon<br />2 horns (E<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>, A, D, B<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>, C, F, E), 2 trumpets (C, D, B<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>), 3 trombones<br />timpani, strings</div>
</dd></dl>
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>
<tr>
